[30;1m29 | [0m[35m    ### Description[0m
[30;1m30 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m31 | [0m[35m    The Mountain Car MDP is a deterministic MDP that consists of a car placed stochastically[0m
[30;1m32 | [0m[35m    at the bottom of a sinusoidal valley, with the only possible actions being the accelerations[0m
[30;1m33 | [0m[35m    that can be applied to the car in either direction. The goal of the MDP is to strategically[0m
[30;1m34 | [0m[35m    accelerate the car to reach the goal state on top of the right hill. There are two versions[0m
[30;1m35 | [0m[35m    of the mountain car domain in gym: one with discrete actions and one with continuous.[0m

[30;1m31 | [0m[35m    The Mountain Car MDP is a deterministic MDP that consists of a car placed stochastically[0m
[30;1m32 | [0m[35m    at the bottom of a sinusoidal valley, with the only possible actions being the accelerations[0m
[30;1m33 | [0m[35m    that can be applied to the car in either direction. The goal of the MDP is to strategically[0m
